   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Legality of cannabis</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       This article is about cannabis as a psychoactive. For information about hemp, see <a href="/wiki/Hemp" title="Hemp">Hemp</a>. For the legalization of hemp in the United States, see <a href="/wiki/Hemp_Farming_Act_of_2018" title="Hemp Farming Act of 2018">Hemp Farming Act of 2018</a>.
      </div> 
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Where cannabis is and is not legal
      </div> 
      <p class="mw-empty-elt"> </p> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg" class="image"><img alt="Map of world cannabis laws for non-medical use" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg/400px-Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="203" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg/600px-Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a5/Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg/800px-Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="2754" data-file-height="1398"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Map-of-world-cannabis-laws.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Legal status of cannabis possession for recreational use</b> 
         <hr> 
         <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r981673959">.mw-parser-output .legend{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid-column}.mw-parser-output .legend-color{display:inline-block;min-width:1.25em;height:1.25em;line-height:1.25;margin:1px 0;text-align:center;border:1px solid black;background-color:transparent;color:black}.mw-parser-output .legend-text{}</style>
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0d00f2; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Legal
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#ffb700; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Illegal but <a href="/wiki/Decriminalized" class="mw-redirect" title="Decriminalized">decriminalized</a>
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#ff9e9e; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Illegal but often <a href="/wiki/Unenforced" class="mw-redirect" title="Unenforced">unenforced</a>
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#ff3c3c; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Illegal
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg" class="image"><img alt="Map of world cannabis laws for medical use" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg/400px-Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="203" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg/600px-Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg/800px-Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="2754" data-file-height="1398"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Map-of-world-medical-cannabis-laws.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div><b>Legal status of cannabis for medical use</b> 
         <hr> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0ea817; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Legal as authorized by a physician
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#0d00f2; color:white; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Legal for any use
         </div> 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r981673959">
         <div class="legend">
          <span class="legend-color" style="background-color:#b8b8b8; color:black; -webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;Illegal
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The <b>legality of <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_(drug)" title="Cannabis (drug)">cannabis</a></b> for <a href="/wiki/Medical_cannabis" title="Medical cannabis">medical</a> and <a href="/wiki/Recreational_drug_use" title="Recreational drug use">recreational</a> use varies by country, in terms of its possession, distribution, and cultivation, and (in regards to medical) how it can be consumed and what medical conditions it can be used for. These policies in most countries are regulated by three <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> treaties: the 1961 <a href="/wiki/Single_Convention_on_Narcotic_Drugs" title="Single Convention on Narcotic Drugs">Single Convention on Narcotic Drugs</a>, the 1971 <a href="/wiki/Convention_on_Psychotropic_Substances" title="Convention on Psychotropic Substances">Convention on Psychotropic Substances</a>, and the 1988 <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Convention_Against_Illicit_Traffic_in_Narcotic_Drugs_and_Psychotropic_Substances" title="United Nations Convention Against Illicit Traffic in Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Substances">Convention Against Illicit Traffic in Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Substances</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> Cannabis is classified as a Schedule I drug under the 1961 treaty;<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> prior to December 2020 it was also included in Schedule IV.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>The use of cannabis for recreational purposes is prohibited in most countries; however, many have adopted a policy of <a href="/wiki/Decriminalization" title="Decriminalization">decriminalization</a> to make simple possession a non-criminal offense (often similar to a minor traffic violation). Others have much more severe penalties such as some Asian and Middle Eastern countries where possession of even small amounts is punished by imprisonment for several years.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> Countries that have legalized recreational cannabis use are <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>, <a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a>, plus 15 states, 2 territories, and the <a href="/wiki/District_of_Columbia" class="mw-redirect" title="District of Columbia">District of Columbia</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Capital_Territory" title="Australian Capital Territory">Australian Capital Territory</a> in <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. Commercial cannabis production and sale is legal nationwide in two countries (Canada and Uruguay) and in all subnational U.S. jurisdictions that have legalized cannabis except Washington, D.C. A policy of limited enforcement has also been adopted in many countries, in particular the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> where the sale of cannabis is tolerated at <a href="/wiki/Coffeeshop_(Netherlands)" title="Coffeeshop (Netherlands)">licensed coffeeshops</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-coffeeshops_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-coffeeshops-6">[6]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Countries that have legalized medical use of cannabis include <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Barbados" title="Barbados">Barbados</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bermuda" title="Bermuda">Bermuda</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chile</a>, <a href="/wiki/Colombia" title="Colombia">Colombia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Croatia" title="Croatia">Croatia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic" title="Czech Republic">Czech Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Denmark" title="Denmark">Denmark</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ecuador" title="Ecuador">Ecuador</a>, <a href="/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>, <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">Ireland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">Italy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">Jamaica</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malawi" title="Malawi">Malawi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Malta</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Macedonia" title="North Macedonia">North Macedonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway">Norway</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a>, <a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">Portugal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines" title="Saint Vincent and the Grenadines">Saint Vincent and the Grenadines</a>, <a href="/wiki/San_Marino" title="San Marino">San Marino</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uruguay" title="Uruguay">Uruguay</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vanuatu" title="Vanuatu">Vanuatu</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zambia" title="Zambia">Zambia</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwe</a>. Others have more restrictive laws that allow only the use of certain cannabis-derived pharmaceuticals, such as <a href="/wiki/Sativex" class="mw-redirect" title="Sativex">Sativex</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marinol" class="mw-redirect" title="Marinol">Marinol</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Epidiolex" class="mw-redirect" title="Epidiolex">Epidiolex</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> In the United States, 35 states and the District of Columbia have legalized the medical use of cannabis, but at the federal level its use remains prohibited for any purpose.<sup id="cite_ref-ncsl_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ncsl-8">[8]</a></sup> </p> 
      <div style="text-align:center;">

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="By_country">By country</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Legality_of_cannabis&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: By country">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

         <td data-sort-value="1.4" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Decriminalized in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Territory" title="Northern Territory">Northern Territory</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Australia" title="South Australia">South Australia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> Legal in <a href="/wiki/Australian_Capital_Territory" title="Australian Capital Territory">Australian Capital Territory</a> for personal use but not for sale.</td> 
         <td data-sort-value="1" style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal at federal level and in all states.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup> Qualifying conditions and other details vary by state.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup></td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_Australia" title="Cannabis in Australia">Cannabis in Australia</a>
          </div> In September 2019, the Australian Capital Territory became the first state or territory of Australia to legalize recreational use of cannabis. Since 31 January 2020 residents have been allowed to grow two plants and possess 50&nbsp;g, though no sales or other transfer is permitted, including cannabis seeds. Federal law also remains enforceable.<sup id="cite_ref-ACT_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ACT-19">[19]</a></sup> </td>

         <td data-sort-value="1" style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal</td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_Colombia" title="Cannabis in Colombia">Cannabis in Colombia</a>
          </div> Decriminalized up to 22&nbsp;g for personal consumption. Individuals carrying greater amounts, or cultivating up to 20 plants, cannot be prosecuted if the drug is for personal use.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[53]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">[55]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">[56]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="background: #ececec; color: #2C2C2C; font-size: smaller; vertical-align: middle; text-align: center;" class="unknown table-unknown">Unknown</td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_North_Korea" title="Cannabis in North Korea">Cannabis in North Korea</a>
          </div> There are conflicting reports on the legal status of cannabis in North Korea. Multiple reports from defectors and tourists claim there is no law regarding the possession of cannabis (as a result, it is not classified as a drug) in North Korea or if there is, it is mostly unenforced. However, other reports claim that cannabis is illegal.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">[126]</a></sup> </td>

         <td data-sort-value="2" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Legal, but access limited to <a href="/wiki/Cannabidiol" title="Cannabidiol">Epidiolex</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dronabinol" title="Dronabinol">Marinol</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nabiximols" title="Nabiximols">Sativex</a> as of now due to the policy implemented by the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Food_and_Drug_Safety" title="Ministry of Food and Drug Safety">Ministry of Food and Drug Safety</a><sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">[127]</a></sup></td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_South_Korea" title="Cannabis in South Korea">Cannabis in South Korea</a>
          </div> Medical use of cannabis was legalized in November 2018. The plant itself, however, remains unavailable due to the policy made by the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Food_and_Drug_Safety" title="Ministry of Food and Drug Safety">Ministry of Food and Drug Safety</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">[128]</a></sup> </td>

           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_Mexico" title="Cannabis in Mexico">Cannabis in Mexico</a>
          </div> Possession of 5&nbsp;g decriminalized since 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">[145]</a></sup> In 2015 the Supreme Court voted 41 that prohibiting people from growing the drug for consumption was unconstitutional, and in 2018 it reaffirmed the ruling.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">[146]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">[147]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">[148]</a></sup> As of November 2020, however, the legislature has still not passed a law to enforce the ruling. The Supreme Court has also constantly extended the legal deadline to pass the legislation.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">[149]</a></sup> </td>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a> </td> 
         <td data-sort-value="1.1" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Consumption and sale are tolerated in licensed <a href="/wiki/Coffeeshop_(Netherlands)" title="Coffeeshop (Netherlands)">coffeeshops</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-coffeeshops_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-coffeeshops-6">[6]</a></sup> Possession of up to 5&nbsp;g is decriminalized. Cultivation of up to 5 plants is unenforced for non-commercial use (unless grown in a professional setup).</td> 
         <td data-sort-value="1" style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal</td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_the_Netherlands" title="Cannabis in the Netherlands">Cannabis in the Netherlands</a>
          </div> Personal possession decriminalized and sale allowed only in certain licensed <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_coffee_shop" class="mw-redirect" title="Cannabis coffee shop">coffeeshops</a> in the continental Netherlands.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">[152]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">[153]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">[154]</a></sup> Cultivation often tolerated but growers can still have their plants and equipment confiscated<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">[155]</a></sup> and face eviction<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">[156]</a></sup> or cancellation of their mortgage<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">[157]</a></sup> for one single plant.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">[158]</a></sup> Zero tolerance policy in the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Netherlands" title="Caribbean Netherlands">Caribbean Netherlands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">[159]</a></sup> </td>

          </div> Banned in 1927.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">[160]</a></sup> Possession over 28 g is <a href="/wiki/Presumption_of_supply_in_New_Zealand" title="Presumption of supply in New Zealand">presumed for supply</a>. Medical use was legalized in 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">[161]</a></sup> In 2020, voters rejected a <a href="/wiki/2020_New_Zealand_cannabis_referendum" title="2020 New Zealand cannabis referendum">referendum to legalize recreational use</a> by a 50.7% to 48.4% margin.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">[162]</a></sup> </td>

         <td data-sort-value="1" style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">[165]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">[166]</a></sup></td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_Norway" title="Cannabis in Norway">Cannabis in Norway</a>
          </div> Illegal, but government is working on a decriminalization bill that would end all sanctions for use and possession of up to 15&nbsp;g. Currently use and possession of up to 15&nbsp;g are punished with heavy fines and possible loss of driver's license.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">[167]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">[168]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">[169]</a></sup> </td>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/12/Flag_of_Poland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Poland.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/12/Flag_of_Poland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Poland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/1/12/Flag_of_Poland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Poland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1280" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Poland" title="Poland">Poland</a> </td> 
         <td data-sort-value="2" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Illegal, but may not be enforced for small amounts, legal below 0.2% THC</td> 
         <td data-sort-value="1" style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal</td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_Poland" title="Cannabis in Poland">Cannabis in Poland</a>
          </div> Since 2011, prosecutors can choose not to prosecute possession of small quantities of cannabis for personal use if it is a first offense or if the person is drug dependent.<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">[182]</a></sup> Possession of large quantities of drugs can result in up to 10 years in prison.<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">[183]</a></sup> </td>

          </div> Possession of small amounts punishable by up to 8 years in prison.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">[201]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-WSJSlovakia_202-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WSJSlovakia-202">[202]</a></sup> In April 2012, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal" title="The Wall Street Journal">The Wall Street Journal</a></i> reported that <a href="/wiki/Robert_Fico" title="Robert Fico">Robert Fico</a>, the incoming Slovak prime minister, might push for partial legalization of cannabis possession, and has argued for the legalization of possession of up to three doses of cannabis for personal use.<sup id="cite_ref-WSJSlovakia_202-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WSJSlovakia-202">[202]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <td data-sort-value="1.2" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Use and possession in private areas allowed for own consumption.<sup id="cite_ref-clubs_games_208-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-clubs_games-208">[208]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">[209]</a></sup> Public possession or consumption can result in a fine from 601 to 30000 .<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">[210]</a></sup> Cultivation for personal use allowed in private areas including <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_Social_Club" title="Cannabis Social Club">Cannabis Social Clubs</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-clubs_games_208-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-clubs_games-208">[208]</a></sup></td> 
         <td data-sort-value="2" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Limited cannabis-derived pharmaceuticals</td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_Spain" title="Cannabis in Spain">Cannabis in Spain</a>
          </div> Cannabis trafficking, including sale, import or cultivation for sale, is punishable by jail time. All actions related to cannabis for own consumption aren't considered criminal offenses,<sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">[211]</a></sup> but misdemeanors punishable by a fine.<sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">[212]</a></sup> Legalized in <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalonia</a> in 2017,<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">[213]</a></sup> but that law was challenged by the state and declared unconstitutional.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">[214]</a></sup> Cultivation in private areas for own consumption is allowed if the plants cannot be seen from the street or other public spaces.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">[215]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

Possessing, purchasing, or receiving any illegal drug is punishable by 12 years of prison, treatment, or probation.<sup id="cite_ref-EMCDDATurkey_235-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EMCDDATurkey-235">[235]</a></sup> Sale and supply is punishable by a prison term of 510 years, and production or trafficking by a minimum term of 10 years.<sup id="cite_ref-EMCDDATurkey_235-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EMCDDATurkey-235">[235]</a></sup> </td>

         <td data-sort-value="3.3" style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal, but a cannabis warning or an on-the-spot fine ("Penalty Notice for Disorder") may be issued for simple possession instead of prosecution.<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">[238]</a></sup></td> 
         <td data-sort-value="1" style="background:#9F9;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-yes">Legal, only when prescribed by a specialist consultant.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_News1_239-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_News1-239">[239]</a></sup></td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="Cannabis in the United Kingdom">Cannabis in the United Kingdom</a>
          </div> Banned in 1928.<sup id="cite_ref-Manning2013_240-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Manning2013-240">[240]</a></sup> Made a Class B drug under the <a href="/wiki/Misuse_of_Drugs_Act_1971" title="Misuse of Drugs Act 1971">Misuse of Drugs Act 1971</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">[241]</a></sup> Limited medical use has been legal since 1 November 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_News2_242-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_News2-242">[242]</a></sup> Cannabis-derived medicines are only legal when prescribed by a specialist consultant and <a href="/wiki/General_practitioner" title="General practitioner">GPs</a> are not allowed to prescribe cannabis-derived medicines. NHS guidance states that medical cannabis should only be prescribed when there is clear published evidence of its benefit and other treatment options have been exhausted.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_News1_239-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_News1-239">[239]</a></sup> </td>

         <td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="650">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> </td> 
         <td data-sort-value="1.3" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Legalized in 15 states, 2 <a href="/wiki/Territories_of_the_United_States" title="Territories of the United States">territories</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">District of Columbia</a>  but illegal at federal level. Decriminalized in another 16 states and 1 territory.
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Decriminalization_of_non-medical_cannabis_in_the_United_States" title="Decriminalization of non-medical cannabis in the United States">Decriminalization of non-medical cannabis in the United States</a>
          </div></td> 
         <td data-sort-value="1.1" style="background:#FFB;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-partial">Legalized in 35 states, 4 territories, and the District of Columbia  but illegal at federal level.<sup id="cite_ref-ncsl_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ncsl-8">[8]</a></sup><br>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           See also: <a href="/wiki/Medical_cannabis_in_the_United_States" title="Medical cannabis in the United States">Medical cannabis in the United States</a>
          </div></td> 
         <td>
          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main articles: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_the_United_States" title="Cannabis in the United States">Cannabis in the United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Legality_of_cannabis_by_U.S._jurisdiction" title="Legality of cannabis by U.S. jurisdiction">Legality of cannabis by U.S. jurisdiction</a>
          </div> Cannabis remains a <a href="/wiki/Controlled_Substances_Act#Schedule_I_controlled_substances" title="Controlled Substances Act">Schedule I drug</a> at federal level, prohibiting even its medical use. The <a href="/wiki/Rohrabacher%E2%80%93Farr_amendment" title="RohrabacherFarr amendment">RohrabacherFarr amendment</a> prevents federal enforcement in states that have legalized medical, however. No such protections exist regarding recreational, but the federal government has so far generally not intervened. Recognized <a href="/wiki/Indian_reservation" title="Indian reservation">Indian reservations</a> are allowed to legalize for either use under a policy announced in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">[243]</a></sup> </td>

          <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
           Main article: <a href="/wiki/Cannabis_in_Venezuela" title="Cannabis in Venezuela">Cannabis in Venezuela</a>
          </div> Possession of up to 20&nbsp;g of marijuana or 5&nbsp;g of genetically modified marijuana for commercial purposes is punishable by 12 years in prison at judge's discretion. If deemed to be for personal consumption, the user is subject to security measures involving rehabilitation and detoxification procedures.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">[249]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="background:#F99;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center;" class="table-no">Illegal</td>
